    SELECT TOP(1) [o].[Id], [o].[City], [o].[Location], [o].[OrderDate], [o].[PhoneNumber], [o].[Status], [o].[TotalAmount], [o].[UserEmail], [o].[UserId]
    FROM [Orders] AS [o]
    WHERE [o].[UserId] = @__foundUserId_0
    ORDER BY [o].[OrderDate] DESC
) AS [o1]
LEFT JOIN [OrderItems] AS [o0] ON [o1].[Id] = [o0].[OrderId]
ORDER BY [o1].[OrderDate] DESC, [o1].[Id]
